I.-INTRODUCTORY_JJ REMARKS_NNP ._.
FOR_IN reasons_NNS that_WDT will_MD appear_VB in_IN the_DT sequel_NN ,_, it_PRP will_MD be_VB in_IN no_DT way_NN necessary_JJ to_TO enter_VB into_IN any_DT separate_JJ description_NN of_IN the_DT maladies_NNS indicated_VBN by_IN the_DT above_JJ popular_JJ terms_NNS ,_, as_IN the_DT main_JJ result_NN of_IN the_DT investigation_NN has_VBZ been_VBN to_TO establish_VB their_PRP$ identity_NN ._.
